The Stolen and Robbed Tongzhou Steamer Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday 129

The Shandong Steamer, Which Transferred Passengers, Also Arrives

Crew Members Describe in Detail the Circumstances of the Robbery

The British-owned Taikoo Company's Northern Seas route Tongzhou steamer, which departed from Shanghai for Yantai and Tianjin on the 28th of last month, was infiltrated by pirates who hijacked the ship outside the Wusongkou. The steamer entered the port at 6:50 AM yesterday and docked at 8:00 AM. A reporter from this newspaper visited the ship yesterday to interview the crew members. The details of the incident are as follows:

Two Steamers Arrive Together 130

When the Tongzhou steamer entered the port yesterday morning, it anchored at Wusongkou. Taikoo's manager, Laimu, notified the Customs, the Water Police Department, and the Municipal Police Bureau Water Police to inspect the ship. This process took half an hour to complete. When the ship arrived in Shanghai and docked at the French Concession wharf at 8:30 AM, detectives from the French Concession Police had already secretly deployed and prohibited idlers from boarding the ship. The Shandong steamer, which transferred the Tongzhou steamer's passengers, also arrived at Wusong yesterday morning and underwent a similar inspection, which was even stricter than the Tongzhou steamer's. After three hours, each passenger was individually checked. As a result, more than ten passengers were taken away by the Water Police Force for further investigation before being released. It was not until 11:00 AM that the steamer was able to dock, and it was subjected to a second inspection. The strictness was unprecedented.

Attempt to Seize New Banknotes 131

The Dapeng Bay pirates had already infiltrated Shanghai at the beginning of January this year. The various shipping companies had been secretly informed in advance by the Hong Kong Police authorities, so the inspection of merchant ships leaving the port was very strict. However, as time passed without any discoveries, they became less vigilant. Little did they know that the pirates had been closely monitoring the movements of various ships in Shanghai. On the 28th of last month, when the Taikoo Company's Tongzhou steamer was heading to Tianjin, the local Bank of China had a batch of newly printed one-yuan, five-yuan, and ten-yuan banknotes, totaling 250,000 yuan, packed in five boxes, to be transported to Tianjin for use in North China. The design of these new banknotes featured an ox plowing the fields. Although the place names and numbers had been compiled, the signatures and seals had not yet been affixed. The original plan was to add the signatures and seals after arriving in Tianjin to ensure prudence. Unexpectedly, the bandits learned of this plan and attempted to seize the banknotes.

Secret Transportation of Firearms 132

Although the Tongzhou steamer was strictly inspected when it left Shanghai last month, the bandits' firearms were not found. After the reporter inquired in detail with the crew members, it was learned that the Tongzhou steamer arrived in Shanghai on the 26th and remained docked for three days. During these three days, many passengers boarded and disembarked. The pirates' firearms were likely secretly transported onto the ship during these three days, when the crowds were noisy, and hidden in places where people could not see them. Therefore, when they boarded the ship as passengers on the 28th, their firearms could not be discovered. There were a total of eleven pirates, including one leader, who was about thirty years old with a dark complexion. After boarding the ship, they dispersed and stayed in the steerage cabins. The bandits claimed that there were twenty-four of them, which was an exaggeration. The steamer departed at 10:00 AM on the 28th. At 6:00 PM that day, when it reached the sea off Sheshan, the bandits launched the robbery.

Control of the Entire Ship 133

At that time, dinner was being served on the ship. The bandit leader seized the opportunity to order his gang to jump out of the steerage cabins, each carrying a pistol and a Mauser pistol, and go straight up to the deck via the staircases on both sides. More than seventy Western adults and children were playing on the deck. The White Russian security guard, seeing this, hurriedly tried to open fire to resist the enemy, but because the bandits were mixed in with the children, he feared causing accidental injury, so he raised his gun but did not fire. The bandit leader took the initiative and shot the Russian guard to death. He also knocked down two engineers before going straight to the bridge, dismantling the radio, and taking the captain into custody. In about two hours, the entire ship was completely under the control of the pirates, who changed course and headed towards South China.

Great Disappointment for the Bandits 134

The pirates' goal was the 250,000 yuan in new banknotes, so after occupying the entire ship, they informed the crew members that they could not leave their cabins unless there was something wrong, in which case they could call for them. They then ordered the crew members to quickly open the bank vault and hand over the banknotes. The crew members, under duress, had no choice but to hand over the five boxes of banknotes. Upon opening them, they saw that they were not signed and knew that they could not be used. The bandit leader was greatly frustrated.

Three Days of Robbery 135

The bandit leader then told the crew members and passengers, "Our hope of not robbing the crew members and passengers has completely failed. You must know that we spent more than 4,000 yuan to come to Shanghai from Hong Kong, and now we have gained nothing. How can we return empty-handed?" He immediately ordered the crew members to hand over all their cash and robbed all the passengers of their belongings. However, the bandit leader informed the bandits that they should not rob women and children by force. In total, the search and robbery began on the morning of the 29th and lasted for three nights and two days. The bandits used the main dining room as their command post, and all the stolen goods were placed in the main dining room.

Maritime Police Officer Dies in the Line of Duty 136

Maritime Police Officer Tihornoff, a White Russian, was shot in the head and died on the deck. Second Engineer Macdonald was shot in the shoulder when he retrieved a pistol from his cabin and came out to resist. The ship had a total of twelve pistols, long guns, and five Mauser pistols, with hundreds of rounds of ammunition, which were used by five maritime police officers and six senior crew members for self-defense, but they were all confiscated by the pirates. The body of the Russian guard who was killed on the second day was thrown into the sea by the pirates. Because the Second Engineer resisted, the pirates wanted to kill him, but after the First Mate repeatedly pleaded with the bandit leader, his life was spared.

Search and Seizure of Cash 137

When the eleven pirates were robbing, they all took off their clothes, wore only single layers, and went barefoot. Before the robbery, the bandit leader had said, "The banknotes cannot be used, please pool together some money." First, they searched the passengers' belongings, and then they went to the compradore's office to confiscate the passenger tickets. The head compradore, Wang Jintao, was not on the ship, but the second compradore, Chen Qinghao, was on board and had no choice but to let them search and rob. There was a female passenger named Mao in the steerage cabin with two children, who only had five dollars on her. The bandit said, "Your travel expenses are too little to go to Tianjin," and ordered the bandits not to rob her, but instead the bandit leader gave her ten dollars. There was also an old woman who was wearing ragged clothes and only had two dollars on her. The bandits also gave her five dollars. The two prostitutes in cabin number nine were found to be selling their bodies for the first time, and the bandit leader ordered the bandits not to rob them. As for the Western children, after consultations with the teachers, they voluntarily pooled together three or four hundred dollars, and they were not searched. As a result of the search and seizure, a total of more than two thousand dollars was obtained.

Two Passengers Lucky 138

There were more than one hundred Chinese passengers on the ship. This time, the bandits' robbery was different from previous robberies. The bandit leader's goal was the banknotes, and he did not value the passengers' and crew members' money. Therefore, during the search and robbery, he did not allow the bandits to act wildly. One bandit was searching a crew member and was more abusive, which was seen by the bandit leader, who punched the bandit to the ground. As a result, many crew members and passengers retained their money. Two passengers carried checks, bank deposit books, and cash, totaling more than 200,000 yuan. They were familiar with the crew members, who temporarily hid them on their behalf. As a result, they were not taken away, which was extremely fortunate.

Forcibly Seizing a Civilian Boat 139

At around 2:00 PM on February 1st, the ship sailed to the sea off Kowloon Mountain near Huizhou, about nine hours' sailing time from Hong Kong. The pirates prepared to leave the ship and blew conch shells on the ship as a signal to find a civilian boat. After a long time, they could not find one. Finally, they discovered a large sailing boat. The pirates ordered it to approach. It turned out that the sailing boat was also a pirate boat, with three men and one woman on board. They had clashed with the Tongzhou steamer pirates. Later, four pirates from the Tongzhou steamer launched a sampan and jumped onto the sailing boat, forcibly detaining it and ordering it to approach the Tongzhou steamer to transport the stolen goods in preparation for carrying them to the Kowloon Mountain side.

Seizing Cargo 140

When the pirates were about to leave, they opened the cargo hold and took out ten boxes of foreign cloth, carrying away dozens of bolts, as well as a box of socks, five barrels of oranges, and a box of candy, all of which were transferred to the sailing boat. There were two bags of mail on the ship, which were also opened by the bandits to check for valuables. As a result, nothing was taken. A postal basket containing 250,000 yuan in postage stamps was torn up by the bandits, but they were not taken away. Although the five boxes of banknotes were not signed, the bandit leader still confiscated them, claiming that he still had a big boss to whom he had to hand them over. The only crew members whose clothes were confiscated were the two compradores, who lost several suits. The bedding of the staff in the accounting office was also taken away.

Abduction Foiled 141

When the pirates left the ship, they originally wanted to abduct seven Chinese passengers as a way to extort ransoms. When the hostages were getting into the sampan, the sailors on the ship told them that the sampan was too small to accommodate so many people. The pirates released three people and only took four people with them. When they arrived at the Kowloon Mountain side, one group of pirates escorted the stolen goods away first, while the other group accompanied the hostages. Fortunately, the British Navy in Hong Kong had received a telegram from the Shanghai company entrusting the Coastal Defense Department to telegram the Hong Kong Navy, requesting a search. Therefore, two aircraft were dispatched, along with one Chinese aircraft, to conduct reconnaissance. The aircraft flew very low, and the pirates were greatly alarmed. They went back on board and dragged the First Mate and a telegraph operator onto the sampan as protective talismans to send them ashore. The sampan arrived at the foot of the mountain, but the pirates, in their panic, overturned the sampan on the seashore.

Aircraft Reconnaissance 142

The aircraft flew close to the ship, clearly observed the situation, and intended to drop bombs. The captain was greatly alarmed because the sampan contained the First Mate and the radio operator. He hurriedly wrote large characters on the ship, asking them not to drop bombs and not to pursue the bandits, to ensure the safety of everyone. The aircraft then left. Seeing that the first sampan had been destroyed, the Tongzhou steamer hurriedly launched another sampan and carried the First Mate, the radio operator, and the passengers back. The radio, which had been dismantled, was also retrieved by the captain from the bandits and reinstalled. Therefore, the Tongzhou steamer departed at about 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the first day.

Old Story Revisited 143

The pirates on the ship told the crew members that the robbery of the Tongzhou nine years ago was also committed by them. The big boss had been replaced, but the brothers were still the same. There were thousands of people in the mountains who depended on this for a living. They also claimed that if they were to rob in Shanghai, their skills would be greater than the local thieves, but they did not want to rob small shops that were making a small profit. The reason they robbed the Tongzhou this time was because they were after the bank's banknotes, because the losses to the bank would be less than those to small shops.

Inspection Upon Arrival in Hong Kong 144

After the bandits left the ship, three British warships arrived to protect the Tongzhou and escort it to Hong Kong. By then, it was already dark, and searchlights were used to indicate the Hong Kong航线. The ship arrived in Hong Kong at 11:00 PM that night. In Hong Kong, the Hong Kong authorities thoroughly inspected all the passengers and dispatched a large number of armed detectives to the ship to be on duty and stationed. It is heard that the Hong Kong government awarded the captain of the Tongzhou a medal for his meritorious service in preserving the lives of the British on board and ensuring that none of the seventy-three children were injured. The injured Second Engineer was immediately sent to the hospital for treatment. The gunshot wound to his shoulder was not life-threatening.

Passengers Transfer Ships 145

All of the Chinese passengers on the ship, totaling one hundred and ten people, transferred to the Shandong steamer in Hong Kong to come to Shanghai. There were twenty-two people in the cabin and eighty-eight people in the steerage. The Western passengers and seventy-three children were still carried by the Tongzhou back to Shanghai. The Tongzhou steamer left Hong Kong on February 2nd and arrived at Wusongkou at 6:46 AM yesterday and at the dock at 8:00 AM. The Shandong steamer arrived at Wusongkou at 7:35 AM yesterday and docked at around 11:00 AM.

Sails Tomorrow 146

The Taikoo Company yesterday notified all the cargo owners and provided a clear notification of the stolen cargo, and notified the Bank of China that all five boxes of new banknotes had been confiscated. The other goods were still on the ship. It is now scheduled to depart for Yantai and Tianjin on the 9th. The seventy-three Western children will still take the original ship to Yantai. A team of British Marines dispatched from Shanghai to Tianjin will take the Tongzhou steamer to Tianjin.

Foreign Newspaper Reports 147

The Greater Shanghai Evening Post reported that after the Taikoo Company's Tongzhou steamer arrived at the Taikoo Wharf in the French Concession at 8:25 AM this morning (the 7th), the British Consul General in Shanghai, Sir Pelham Laird Warren, and the British Shipping Consul, Lamb, boarded the ship for a non-public inspection less than an hour later, at around 9:00 AM. It is expected that the inspection can be completed in two days. This time, unlike

Repeat Offenders of Using Potent Narcotics to be Executed 148

A proclamation issued by the Songhu Garrison Command states: "It has been received from Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission on January 30th of this year: "Upon reviewing Article 5 of the Regulations on the Strict Prohibition of Potent Narcotics, which stipulates that anyone who has been taken into custody by government authorities and ordered to undergo medical treatment for a specified period to quit the habit, but who repeats the use of potent narcotics, shall be executed. This is to eradicate the atmosphere of drug use and severely punish repeat offenders. The same law shall apply to those who voluntarily surrender themselves to request rehabilitation but relapse. However, because the law has not been clearly defined, provinces and cities have been seeking clarification. After reviewing and approving the measures, it has been decided that anyone who is addicted to drugs, voluntarily surrenders themselves to request rehabilitation, and is given a certificate by the government authorities, and who submits a written pledge that they will be executed if they relapse and is released, shall be treated as if they had been taken into custody, ordered to undergo medical treatment, and relapsed, and shall be dealt with in accordance with the latter part of Article 5 of the regulations. Those whose circumstances of the crime are pitiable and excusable may be granted a reduction in sentence in accordance with the law. You are to comply with this and inform all subordinates." In addition to issuing orders, this proclamation is hereby issued to inform the public."

Ten years ago, after the ship encountered pirates, the naval court conducted a public inspection. The British authorities feel that a non-public inspection can gain more insights and be completed more quickly. The ship is scheduled to depart for Yantai on Saturday morning with the original passengers. The children on board will temporarily stay with relatives and friends. The China Inland Mission is scheduled to hold a tea party tomorrow afternoon at 4:00 PM to entertain them.

New Check Clearing Method Revised by the Joint Reserve Board of Banks 149

To be Implemented from February 8th

The Joint Reserve Board of Banks in this city has found that in recent times, interbank remittances between the head offices and branch offices of various banks in other locations often use credit letters or three-part credit slips instead of bank drafts. The nature of these instruments is quite different from the entrustment payment documents other than bank-specified instruments. The payment methods still need to be standardized to ensure uniformity. It is understood that this issue has been resolved at the 16th meeting of the Check Clearing House Committee of the Association, which has formulated the following payment methods for credit letters or credit slips that are in the nature of bank drafts: (1) The remittance credit letters or three-part credit slips used between the head offices and branch offices of each clearing bank must have the words "For Clearing" stamped on the face of the instrument, otherwise it will be regarded as a return item. (2) Each clearing bank should immediately notify its branch offices in other locations that all silver dollar credit letters or credit slips issued for clearing must have the words "For Clearing" stamped on them. (3) The payment methods for remittance credit letters or credit slips issued by entities other than the clearing banks and their branch offices shall continue to be handled according to the original practices of each bank. It is heard that these measures will be implemented from (the 8th).

The Two Railways Administration Sends Personnel to England to Supervise the Construction of Locomotives 150

Zhong Yangqi Scheduled to Leave the Country on the 13th

The Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway previously leased locomotives from the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway. Subsequently, it was determined that the locomotives would be of the 4-8-4 type, which would be manufactured in England. For the sake of prudence, the Ministry of Railways previously appointed Ying Shangfang, a commissioner of the Technical Standards Committee, to go to England to be stationed at the factory to liaise, guide the design, and supervise the construction. Considering the special cargo transport conditions and bridge load limits of the railway, the Two Railways Administration requested and was granted approval from the Ministry of Railways to specially appoint Zhong Yangqi, a mechanical engineer and the head of the design section of the Engineering Department of the Machinery Department, to go to England to monitor the manufacturing along with Commissioner Ying. Chief Zhong is scheduled to leave the country by ship on the 13th of this month and is expected to be stationed in England for about seven months. Afterwards, he will take the opportunity to visit locomotive factories and locomotive depots on various railways in England for two or three months to gain experience.

The Two Railways Administration Continues to Send Old Uniforms to Aid Disaster Relief 151

The Two Railways Administration previously collected old uniforms from various departments within the bureau to help with disaster relief due to the severe drought in various provinces last year. The first batch was sent to the Shanghai Disaster Relief Association for various drought-stricken provinces on the 15th of last month to be distributed on its behalf. More old uniforms have now been collected, including 1,177 black wool uniforms, 43 pairs of black wool trousers, 2,065 yellow cloth uniforms, 6 pairs of yellow cloth trousers, 1,207 pairs of black leather shoes, 827 yellow cloth hats, 835 yellow leather belts, 671 pairs of leggings, and 960 black wool hats. New Quarantine Hospital Built by the Port Quarantine Office is Completed 152

Located at the Former Site of the Wusong Seashore Hotel

Features an Observation Deck with Views of Approaching Ships

Infected Passengers Will Be Kept There for Examination and Treatment

The Port Quarantine Administration believes that the number of ships entering and leaving the port in this city is increasing daily, and the quarantine work must also be actively intensified. Therefore, it has built the most modern quarantine hospital at Wusong, which is now completed. In the future, when infected passengers are found on incoming ships, they can be isolated and treated there, and disinfection can be carried out. As the matter is important, a reporter from the Datong News Agency has recorded the situation as follows:

New Quarantine Hospital 153

The Port Quarantine Administration already has a quarantine hospital in Pudong, which was received from the Customs Office. However, the equipment is no longer modern, and its location is somewhat remote. Therefore, it purchased the old site of the Wusong Seashore Hotel to build the most modern quarantine hospital. Now that the hospital site has been completed, it can be opened and isolation, examination, and treatment can be implemented as soon as the equipment is installed.

Internal Observation Tower 154

Medical equipment includes isolation wards, quarantine rooms, clothing disinfection rooms, bathhouses, and so on. At the same time, an observation tower, 56 feet high, has been rebuilt in the hospital compound to observe incoming ships outside the Wusong estuary. It is said that by climbing the tower and looking into the distance, the masts and sails of ships within tens of miles can be seen at a glance, which is especially effective in assisting quarantine work.

Importance of the Nature 155

According to Zhou Zhongqian, Secretary of the Quarantine Administration, the new-style quarantine hospital will soon be completed in terms of equipment. In the future, travelers infected with the epidemic will be kept there for isolation and treatment, so as not to delay the import time of ships. At the same time, because the hospital is equipped with an observation tower, ships coming to Shanghai with yellow flags can also be seen in advance, and medical officers can be dispatched to inspect the ships quickly, which is more convenient.

County Government Announces Re-extension of Halved Deed Tax for Three Months 156

Starting from February

The Shanghai County Government has received an order from the provincial government that the deed tax on fields and houses, which was originally levied at 9.6%, has been reduced to 6.3% from September of the 23rd year, limited to three months. It has been extended twice for three months, and will expire at the end of January of this year. It should have been terminated and no longer extended. However, after last year's drought, the people's conditions were dilapidated and material resources were difficult. Those who established deeds for buying fields and houses before could not pay taxes within the time limit everywhere. If the reduction and collection are not extended again, it is feared that it will cause wait-and-see attitudes and lose the purpose of enriching taxes and caring for the people. Now, starting from February of this year, the reduced tax rate of 6.3% will be extended for another three months. The original collection of surcharges and Chinese-funded donations will still be reduced in proportion to the previous case, so as to reduce the burden, etc. After the county government received the order, in addition to ordering the public offices in each district, township, and town to comply with it, it also announced it to the whole county for everyone to know.

Ministry of Finance Instructs on Methods for Guarantee Money for Savings Deposits 157

Based on the Total Savings Amount of the Previous Year's Final Accounts

A Nanjing telegram states that the Shanghai Banking Association sent a letter to the Savings Deposit Custody Committee, inquiring about the methods for paying guarantee money in the second half of the 23rd year. The Custody Committee requested instructions from the Ministry of Finance. The Ministry of Finance replied on the 7th that the amount payable by each bank and association should be based on the total amount of savings deposits at the time of the previous year's final accounts. After verification, the case will be compiled and notified.

Ministry of Finance Hands Over for Discussion Subsidies for Shanghai's Affordable Housing 158

Nanjing Telephone, the Shanghai Municipal Government previously raised the issue of expensive land prices in Shanghai, which caused problems for ordinary people to live in. It plans to raise funds to build many affordable housing units in various sections of northern Shanghai. Recently, it continues to build many affordable housing units in the Shanghai Siyi area, with a budgeted cost of more than one million yuan. It has submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to find ways to allocate funds for subsidies. The Ministry of Finance has handed it over to the department for review.

The Bank of China Agrees to Study and Prepare

Nanjing Telegram, According to repeated suggestions from national goods merchants in Manila, requesting the government to urge domestic banks to establish overseas branches, the Ministry of Finance is now dividing the nature of banks into three categories: the Central Bank as a national bank, the Bank of China as a foreign exchange bank, and the Bank of Communications as an industrial bank. After the Ministry of Finance forwarded it to the Bank of China for investigation and handling, the bank replied that it would study and prepare at any time and strive to achieve it.

Conclusion of the Wu Fushun Suspected of Wife Murder Case 162

Changes After Zhu Xiaomei's Disappearance

Wu Fushun (39 years old), a local, has lived near the left side of Wujia Land Tang in Pudong since he was a child, and made a living by farming. In the past, he married a wife, Ms. Lu, and had a son named Longsheng, who has already married. Ms. Lu died of illness. In June of last year, Sun Jiangshi, Chen Ashun, and others acted as matchmakers for Wu Fushun to remarry Zhu Xiaomei (43 years old), a Chongming woman, as a successor. Since Xiaomei passed the door, the couple still showed affection. Unexpectedly, only two months after the marriage, Sun Jiangshi, Chen Ashun, and others suddenly came to Wu's house and declared that they would go to Shanghai together, on the grounds of watching a play, and took Xiaomei out with them. Since then, she has never returned. More than ten days later, unexpectedly, a female corpse was found in a flower field of a certain surname about five miles away from Wu's house. The police station in charge reported to the local court and sent personnel to verify that the female corpse was indeed Zhu Xiaomei, who had been missing for more than ten days, and was murdered and abandoned there. Wu Fushun was in a suspicious position and was sent to the court by the police station. Prosecutor Lei Binzhang questioned and ruled to detain him, and prosecuted the criminal court with murder. At 2 pm yesterday, Judge Guan Liting specially opened the 10th court for trial, ordering Wu Fushun, who was in custody, to be brought to the case for a long time of investigation, and Prosecutor Lei made a plea. Then, the appointed lawyer Zhou Yuqi defended him and requested to declare him not guilty. The judge considered the conclusion and decided to pronounce the verdict on the 13th of this month. Wu Fushun was sent back to custody.

Mei Lanfang Talks About His Trip to Russia 163

Due to the Change of Route, I Had to Decline the Japanese Hospitality

The reporter interviewed Mr. Mei Lanfang, who is about to go to Russia, the day before yesterday. According to Mr. Mei, what people often ask about my trip to Russia is nothing more than 1) the route problem and 2) who will be traveling with me. I will now inform you of the latest decisions below.

Route to Russia 164

Because the Soviet Union telegraphed at the time to take the Siberian train to Moscow, I had to go to Vladivostok from Shanghai. Because Russian ships have no fixed schedule, and the Cultural Association agreed to arrive in Moscow before March 15, it is planned to change the route to Japan, from Kobe to Tsuruga to Vladivostok, in order to be simple and quick. This ticket has been booked. However, recently, the Soviet Union sent another telegram saying that it had decided to send a special ship from Vladivostok to Shanghai to meet Ambassador Yan and myself. Because the Soviet government is so generous, it decided to change the route and take the ship with Ambassador Yan to Vladivostok. The name of the special ship sent by the Russian side has not yet been telegraphed from Vladivostok, but it is known that the departure date from Shanghai is approximately between February 18th, 19th and 25th of the week.

Commemorative Monument to the Martyrs of Jiangwan (January 28th) 166

More Than 1,300 Patriotic Souls Who Died for Their Country

Patriots Donate Funds Separately to Accomplish This

Guomin News Agency reported that the reporter took the opportunity of the January 28th commemoration to visit the January 28th Martyrs Cemetery organized by Jiangwan Chongshan Hall. The cemetery covers an area of 10 mu and contains more than 1,300 bodies of soldiers and civilians who died in the Shanghai War. According to the person in charge of the hall, the coffin and burial expenses were donated by Mr. Wang Weiguan, general manager of Delong Tobacco Company, and the directors Cai Xiangsun and others donated funds for the burial. Recently, after the burial was completed, in order to leave a permanent memorial to comfort the souls of the martyrs, a monument was built in front of the tomb. The cost was donated by Yan Enzhang, the former director of the Diplomatic Office in Shanghai. A memorial archway was also built at the entrance, and the plaques have been submitted to famous figures of the Party and the country for inscription, in order to show respect. The project was designed by architect Quan Renyuan and constructed by Cai Hongji Shuimu, requiring a total of more than 2,000 yuan in silver. It is expected that the entire project can be completed by the end of March this year. Currently, the Municipal Engineering Bureau has submitted a request to the municipal government to build the January 28th Martyrs Cemetery Memorial Road from Yueshi Bridge to the Martyrs Cemetery, and the road plan has been surveyed and will be built soon to facilitate transportation. The reporter also asked whether the tomb was the same as the Tomb of Anonymous Heroes. According to the reply, the Tomb of Anonymous Heroes is located in Miaohang and was initiated and built by famous figures in Shanghai. There are no bodies in the tomb, only a tomb for people to admire, and the scale is very large, with a construction cost of 240,000 yuan, which is completely different from the Martyrs Cemetery.

Four Robbers Sentenced 172

Robbing Repeatedly in the Baseball Field Area

Committing As Many As Sixteen Consecutive Cases

The four robbers, Yang Xiaobao, Chen Xiaosizi, Chen Youqing, and Yang Tongguo (nicknamed Yang Tonggu), from Jiangbei, are all brothers and relatives. They used to make a living by pulling rickshaws. Last winter, due to the difficulty of life, they changed their occupation to street robbers. They used the section of the French Concession from Saposai Road's Père Hilaire to Kangdi Road, which is located in a remote area and has only baseball fields on both sides, with no residents and few people, as an opportunity. They would lie in ambush in the Cangqiao Lane next to the Public Works Department's Lihua Children's Public School, waiting for passersby to pass by, and then come out to rob their property. Late on the night of the third of last month, the detectives of the French patrol house, Zhou Ruzhang and Gao Hongxuan, first captured the two bandits, Yang Xiaobao and Chen Xiaosizi, in the area and escorted them to the Second Special Court for interrogation and detention. At midnight on the tenth of the same month, the detective of the French patrol house, Zhang Ziying, passed in front of the Public Works Department's Chinese Children's Public School and suddenly encountered two bandits who rushed out of a small alley to rob. Zhang pretended to reach into his pocket to take out money, pulled out his pistol, and ordered them to raise their hands. The two bandits were startled and surrendered. They were taken into the patrol house, and their names were Chen Youqing and Yang Tongguo. They were accomplices of the Yang and Chen bandits who were previously captured. The next day, they were escorted to the court for interrogation and combined investigation. The details have been recorded in the previous newspaper. Subsequently, the patrol house found that the bandits had committed as many as sixteen consecutive robbery cases in the section of Saposai Road and elsewhere. Late on the night of the fourth of the same month, they robbed Xu Xin, an officer of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, of cash and ornaments. Later, because the victim was robbed and had no money, he could not go home. The bandits gave the victim a small foreign coin worth two jiao and instructed him to take a rickshaw home. The detectives in charge, Zhou Ruzhang, and others, investigated the case, transferred the victim to retrieve the stolen goods, and sent them to the court's police department, prosecuting them for continuous robbery. Judge Zhang Chaozu tried and concluded the case. The day before yesterday, Judge Zhang opened the court and sentenced Chen Youqing and Yang Tongguo to eight years of imprisonment each, Yang Xiaobao to seven years of imprisonment, and Chen Xiaosizi to three years and six months of imprisonment. After the sentence was passed, the defendants were transferred to the detention center to wait for the appeal period before being sent to prison.

Regulations of the Shanghai Municipal Council on Rickshaws: A Summary of Developments 173

The Shanghai Municipal Council’s Rickshaw Management Committee was formed in early May of last year. Recently, the committee chairman, Mr. Massey, reported to the Board of Directors on the progress of work during the past year. A summary is recorded below:

Registering Genuine Rickshaw Owners: The primary task of the Rickshaw Committee was to conduct rickshaw owner registration. Previously, the 9,990 rickshaw licenses were registered under the names of 144 individuals, leading to illegal resale of licenses. After the owner registration, only the owners themselves could obtain the licenses. After the announcement, rickshaw owners came to register enthusiastically. Later, due to obstruction from the Rickshaw Owners Association, owner certificates could not be issued as scheduled. Subsequently, the Bureau announced that from August onward, rickshaws without owner certificates would no longer be able to obtain operating licenses, and the vacancies would be filled by new applicants. At one point, there were 4,894 applicants requesting a total of over 47,000 rickshaws. Later, the old rickshaw owners were willing to handle the matter according to the agreed-upon method, and the new applicants had no licenses to be allocated. The Rickshaw Committee then conducted a detailed review of the qualifications of the old rickshaw owners who requested registration, and as a result, issued 1,080 owner certificates. Since August, the licenses for the vehicles have been issued entirely based on the owner certificates to the genuine rickshaw owners.

Establishing Standard Rickshaw Rental Rates: The second important task of the Rickshaw Committee was to reduce rickshaw rental rates and establish standards. This was approved by the Board of Directors on August 7th. Subsequently, the rickshaw rental rate was set at 78 cents (dollars) per day. According to previous investigations, the rental rate had been as high as $1.10, which was quite beneficial to the rickshaw pullers. However, monitoring compliance with the rickshaw rental standard was very difficult, as the rental was not for the entire day but in shifts, and the rickshaw owners also collected debts and rent from the rickshaw pullers, resulting in unclear accounts. The Rickshaw Committee has ordered that all extra income be recorded in separate accounts for inspection at any time. However, the greatest difficulty was that the rickshaw pullers dared not confront the rickshaw owners directly, fearing that offending the rickshaw owners would result in no rickshaws to pull. Therefore, the Rickshaw Committee could only implement supervision through other methods, and if necessary, revoke or withhold licenses as punishment. As for the rickshaw rental amount, it should be reduced to 80 cents in small coins (approximately 60 cents in silver dollars) in the future.

Registration of Chartered Rickshaw Pullers: The next step for the Rickshaw Committee was to register all rickshaw pullers, requiring them to comply with regulations and obtain licenses. Starting on September 1st of last year, registration began for private rickshaws (chartered rickshaws). The registration method involved first examining knowledge of traffic regulations, then conducting physical examinations and testing hearing and vision. Then, photos were taken, fingerprints recorded, and vaccinations or inoculations were administered. Lecturers explained matters to be noted when pulling rickshaws. After completion, licenses and armbands were issued. In November, an agreement was reached with the French Concession authorities to make licensing of chartered rickshaw pullers mandatory. From November 1st, those without licenses would no longer be allowed to pull rickshaws. By the end of the year, all chartered rickshaw pullers had been registered, totaling 13,262 people. The registration fee was one dollar per person. Licensing of Public Rickshaw Pullers: The original plan was to register a total of 40,000 rickshaw pullers for public rickshaws, with 30,000 recommended by rickshaw owners, and the Shanghai Municipal Council selecting another 10,000. If registration progressed satisfactorily, the remaining 10,000 might also be recommended by rickshaw owners. Since November, blank forms have been distributed to rickshaw owners, and registration began in December. A total of over 5,800 people have been processed, with approximately rejected as unqualified. The registration procedure is the same as for chartered rickshaw pullers. However, during the lectures, it is specifically explained that although recommended by rickshaw owners, there is no , and they are also informed of the organization of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society and its work, and the registration fee has already been paid by the society on their behalf.

Promoting Model New Rickshaws: For the sake of cleanliness and safety of rickshaws, the Rickshaw Committee specifically set the standard for rickshaws. However, rickshaw owners had many objections. By the end of December, 20 of these standard rickshaws had been licensed and put into operation. By the end of January this year, there would be 150. Together, the main force had accumulated unused materials from old-style rickshaws, which were said to be enough to build a much. The Rickshaw Committee then allowed that if rickshaw owners cooperate fully with registration, they could use these old-style new rickshaws for replacement.

Establishing Mutual Aid Association Affairs: For the sake of the rickshaw pullers, the Rickshaw Committee promoted the organization of a Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Society. The source of the association fees is collected from the rickshaw pullers by the rickshaw owners, with each rickshaw owner initially advancing $1.50 per rickshaw per month. Social figures who express sympathy and are willing to contribute are also welcome. As for its organization, the Shanghai Municipal Council appoints three members to the fund committee, and a board of directors is established, inviting seven enthusiastic people from society, together with two representatives from the rickshaw owners and the three members of the fund committee, to jointly preside over the affairs. Once the rickshaw pullers are registered, they will immediately elect representatives to join the board of directors. The purpose of the Mutual Aid Society is to provide rickshaw pullers with medical care, bathhouses, housing, schools, cooperatives, savings societies, as well as entertainment and aid for injuries and deaths. Now that it has just begun, it is temporarily setting up a center in the northern and northwestern districts, with the general headquarters located on Dongjiaxing Road, occupying 16,000 square feet, with a rooftop garden of the same area. It is expected to officially open in February. The directors of the board of directors are all fully committed. The income from donations to the Mutual Aid Society, in addition to the $40,000 needed for rickshaw puller registration fees, is used for business expenses and the salaries of required staff. The rickshaw pullers' donations are approximately 11 copper coins per shift. Now that rickshaw rentals have been reduced, this amount should not be difficult to bear.

Other Work Last Year: There were also items such as setting fare tables, improving rickshaw lights, revising license regulations, and cracking down on illegal chartered rickshaws. As for the French Concession and the municipal government, the Rickshaw Committee cooperates whenever possible. However, it is hoped that in the future, all three municipal districts will issue rickshaw licenses directly to the rickshaw owners. Regarding the Rickshaw Committee's work in 1935, there will be no problem with its progress, and its development will depend on the attitude of the rickshaw owners. However, the Shanghai Municipal Council's established policy is to improve the situation of rickshaw pullers and improve the condition of rickshaws. This is something that the general public should know.

The Ministry of Interior Issues an Order Strictly Prohibiting Ineffective Smallpox Vaccine 174

Kirin, Triangle, Sino-Western, and Longevity Brands

The Ministry of Interior considers the quality of smallpox vaccine to be of utmost importance in the prevention of smallpox. Upon investigation, the Kirin, Triangle, Sino-Western, and Longevity brands of smallpox vaccine sold in Hankou City were found to be ineffective after testing. It has already issued an order to the relevant authorities in all provinces and cities to strictly prohibit their sale. Other commercially available smallpox vaccines are also ordered to be carefully inspected at any time to eliminate malpractices and achieve the effect of vigorously implementing vaccination. It is reported that the Shanghai Municipal Government has received the notification and will strictly inspect the smallpox vaccines sold in the city. If there are any that do not comply with the provisions of the Chinese Pharmacopoeia regarding the clearly stated expiration date, they should be destroyed and fined in accordance with the Regulations for the Management of Pharmacists.

Retrial of Zhang Guanghua's Case of Killing His Younger Brother Concludes with Closing Arguments 177

Guanghua Still Absolutely Denies It, Sentencing Scheduled for the 13th

Zhang Guanghua, a Henan native living in a three-story pavilion room at 24 Chongde Lane, Minguo Road, outside Xiaobeimen, French Concession, allegedly killed his younger brother Zhang Guangzhou on the evening of November 22nd of last year. Guanghua also suffered knife wounds to his head. The case was transferred by the French Police Department to the Special No. 2 Court, and a public prosecution was filed for the crime of murder. Judge Xiong Huiping repeatedly held hearings and personally visited the scene of the incident. Zhang Guanghua repeatedly denied killing his younger brother in court and hired a lawyer to defend him. Closing arguments have been announced, and sentencing was scheduled. Later, due to lingering doubts in the case, Judge Xiong specially revoked the closing arguments out of prudence and waited for a retrial to be scheduled. Details of the reopening of closing arguments have been reported previously. At 3:00 pm yesterday, Judge Xiong, accompanied by Secretary Tao Zongkan, specially opened the Criminal Court No. 2 for trial. Lawyer Fei Xizhen represented the Police Department in court, and the defense lawyer hired by the defendant also arrived on time. The official ordered the defendant Zhang Guanghua to be brought before the court and said to Zhang, "According to what you previously said, you couldn't see the face of the murderer at the time of the incident. You only saw the murderer cut you and then cut your brother's bed. Now, after detailed review of the testimony of various witnesses and the investigation by the Police Department, and after this court went to your residence to see, the comprehensive review is inconsistent with your various statements in fact. Moreover, after you were injured, you jumped out of the window because you couldn't open the door, and shouted to open the window of Yan Jintao on the second floor to enter. Your door was tightly closed, so how could a third person come in? According to the testimony of witness Yan Jintao, only the sound of you jumping out was heard, and there was no sound of a second person escaping. Moreover, the murder weapon in the case was, according to you, your own, placed under the bed. So how could the murderer calmly take the knife and kill? Judging from all the circumstances, it is true that your brother first held a knife and cut you, and you took the knife and cut back. You should tell the truth." Zhang replied, "My brother and I have always been on good terms. He was very obedient to me. There is no way I would kill my younger brother. If I killed my younger brother, there must be blood stains to prove it. There are no blood stains now. Please be clear." The official also said, "According to what you said, your brother and you have no feud with anyone, no affair, and no intention of robbery. Why did such a tragedy happen?" Zhang replied, "I don't know." The official also said, "According to the circumstances of this case, if you can prove that there was a third person in the room besides you and your brother, there is still something to say. Moreover, the bedding in your room was neat and not messy. This point is enough to prove that your brother cut you first, and you took the knife and cut back. If your brother committed suicide after cutting you, there is no way he would have the strength to cut his own neck." Zhang still categorically denied killing his brother, saying that he had already escaped outside, and he did not know the situation in the room. The official also summoned Qiu Changsheng, Hua Constable No. 455 of the French Concession Police Department, to testify, saying that he was on the preparatory shift that night. They first reported to the police station, and then he went with two detectives. They entered through the back door. The detectives were in front, and he was behind on the stairs. Because he couldn't open the door, he kicked the door open. He saw that the person in the room was already dead, so he closed the door tightly and told them not to enter. At this point, after the secretary read the minutes, the court immediately ordered the start of closing arguments and then announced the adjournment. Sentencing was scheduled for the 13th, and the defendant was still detained pending instructions.

The Bureau of Public Safety Orders All Branches to Effectively Crack Down on the Addition of Mezzanines 178

Not Only Harmful to Cleanliness and Hygiene

A Fire Can Occur with a Moment's Carelessness

The Director of the Municipal Bureau of Public Safety, Wen Chaoji, yesterday received a letter from the Municipal Party Department, stating that (according to a report from the 16th Branch, forwarded by the 4th District Party Department, the buildings in this city are mostly one-story with a kitchen, pavilion, and sun deck, etc. However, landlords often build a second floor mezzanine to divide the front and back of the building, a total of four floors including the upstairs and downstairs mezzanine pavilion, and rent it to three tenants. However, with little space and many people, it is extremely detrimental to hygiene and public order. Moreover, some sun decks that only allow air and sunlight are covered with five-story sheds. Therefore, items such as laundry have to be hung out on the street. This city is a district where Chinese and foreigners gather. This phenomenon is not only harmful to cleanliness and hygiene, but also detrimental to international views. This should be cracked down on, one. Secondly, a fire can occur with a moment's carelessness. According to Western-style architecture, if a house catches fire, it cannot spread to another house. However, the materials of these five-story sheds are all wooden pillars and planks. If house A catches fire, it will spread to house B. And every time a fire is seen, it is mostly mediated by the five-story shed. Every time it is seen that rescue is rapid, the upstairs and downstairs of house B are often not burned, but the five-story shed is already burned out. It has been found that those who rent these multi-story sheds are mostly hard-working people who are greedy for low rents. Once burned in a fire, they are left with nothing, which is very regrettable. This should be cracked down on, two. For this reason, it is appropriate to submit a document to your committee for review and approval, and then forward it to the higher authorities to request the Bureau of Public Works and the Bureau of Public Safety to prohibit the repair of existing five-story sheds and allow them to disappear naturally. New buildings and buildings that have not been built with five-story sheds will not be issued permits in the future, so as to avoid the danger of fire and take care of the livelihood of the people, etc. It is now learned that after reviewing the letter, the bureau, in addition to informing the Bureau of Public Works, has also issued an order to all branch teams to effectively crack down on it.

Cracking Down on Underage Boys Pulling Rickshaws 182

Refusing to Rent to the Elderly and Weak

Those Who Violate Will Be Severely Punished Upon Detection

In this city, there are often underage boys who pull rickshaws for a living, which not only hinders their physical development, but also poses a danger to passengers. Someone has requested the Municipal Bureau of Public Safety to issue an order to prohibit it. Now, it is learned that after receiving the request, the bureau has yesterday sent a letter to the Bureau of Public Utilities, ordering all rickshaw owners to refuse to rent to the elderly, weak, and underage rickshaw pullers until the problem of relieving unemployed rickshaw pullers is resolved. If any rickshaw owner fails to comply, they will be severely punished upon detection. At the same time, an order has been issued to all branches and police stations to strictly enforce the "Regulations on Penalties for Banning Operating Rickshaws" and to copy and report the location, time, and rickshaw number to the bureau for verification.

The Bureau of Public Health Convenes a Meeting to Prohibit the Dumping of Feces into Ditches 183

Ordering Contractors to Effectively Rectify

Prohibiting Feces Cart Drivers from Illegal Extortion

Feces cart drivers in this city have been illegally extorting money from households and often dumping feces into ditches. Although the authorities have repeatedly cracked down on this, it is difficult to prohibit. Recently, someone claiming to be a representative of the feces carts distributed printed materials from the Shanghai South District Agricultural Feces Transport Cart Households to various residents, stating that each bucket would be charged 30 copper coins per day. They went to extort money from Xu and others at 70 Nong, Dengyun Bridge, Hongqiao Tou, in the city. When they believed that the payment was not based on any legal basis and refused to pay, the feces cart drivers threatened to not empty the bedpans. Therefore, they filed a complaint with the municipal government and were allowed to order the relevant bureaus to discuss and formulate effective methods of restraint. After receiving the report, the municipal government ordered the Director of the Bureau of Public Health, Li Tingan, to handle it. It is now learned that after receiving the order, Director Li convened a meeting of officials from the relevant agencies in the city at the bureau at 3:00 pm yesterday. In addition to Jiang Shicheng, representing the Bureau of Public Health, Ni Zuwang from the Bureau of Finance, Lin Ganqing from the Bureau of Public Works, Xiao賀昌 from the Bureau of Public Utilities, Wu Huanru from the Bureau of Social Affairs, Xiao, the Director of the Security Section of the Bureau of Public Safety, and Yi, the Director of the Traffic Section, and other representatives, seven people in total, Jiang Shicheng was elected chairman and the meeting was held as scheduled. First, the chairman reported the purpose of the meeting, and then the discussion began. (1) Ordering contractors to effectively rectify, on the one hand, the Bureau of Public Safety and the Bureau of Public Health will send personnel to conduct strict investigations, and those who violate will be punished. (2) Those who repeatedly fail to reform will have their contracts cancelled, on the one hand, the feces cart drivers who dump feces will be detained and punished, and the association will be ordered to expel them. (3) Prohibiting feces cart drivers from illegal extortion, the meeting adjourned at 4:00 pm.

Manager of Xieji Silk Weaving Factory Accused of Embezzlement 188

Zhu Yaokun Posts 15,000 Yuan Shop Guarantee

The Xieji Silk Weaving Factory, located at No. 51, Lane 465, Xiaoshadu Road, West Shanghai, was jointly established by Zhu Xinru, Zhu Yaokun, and three others. It has been in operation for six years since its opening in 1928. Business was considered to be developing well. At that time, Zhu Xinhe was appointed as general manager and Zhu Yaokun as manager. However, at the end of last year, when Zhu Xinhe went to the factory to check the accounts, he discovered that Zhu Yaokun was suspected of embezzling 27,000 yuan. He then retained lawyer Chen Tingrui to report to the Gordon Road Police Station, who dispatched detective Zhu Mengwei and Western detective Moore to arrest Zhu Yaokun at No. 14, Shenxin Lane, Route du Père Robert, in the French Concession. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. The defendant retained lawyer E Sen to defend him in court. First, police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the case, prosecuting according to Article 357 of the Criminal Law for occupational embezzlement. Following this, Zhu Xinru submitted a statement, stating that the defendant was suspected of embezzling 27,000 yuan, and declaring that the actual amount embezzled could not be determined at the moment. Currently, it has only been found that the Zhenyi Hao shop in the Nine Acres area of the South City has paid 13,352 yuan and 95 cents, which has already been paid, but the defendant did not register it in the disaster relief ledger. The defendant's personal seal was found on the Zhenyi receipt book, so they requested permission for an extension to continue checking the accounts. When questioned, the defendant denied embezzling any money, and declared that Zhu Xinru was an honorary general manager and never interfered with factory affairs. This time, he suddenly took away the account books and fabricated accounts, and sent him to the police station on New Year's Eve. He requested an investigation, and his agent, lawyer E Sen, requested permission to post bail so that he could go out to investigate the accounts. Judge Wu Tingqi verified the confession and ordered Zhu Yaokun to post a shop guarantee of 15,000 yuan and adjourned the hearing to February 14th.

Gambling Case at Dafang Hotel Judgement 189

Fines Imposed on All Parties

The Dafang Hotel, located at No. 33 Zhengjia Wood Bridge Street in the French Concession, and opened by Ningbo native Shen Yongkang, rented out rooms 236 on the second floor to local Shanghai residents led by Yin Bota, 25 years old and residing at 594 Tangshan Road engaged in the old goods business, to gamble and profit by taking a cut. This was discovered by the French Concession police gambling squad, including detective Su Erchai, deputy Bingquan, Lu Changsheng, and detectives Li Zongyi and Chen Yishan, who rushed to the scene at 12:30 AM and arrested gamblers including Yin Boqing, Huang Shuyu, Sun Zeshi, Lu Zongxiang, Yu Defu, Li Jiajun, Wang Jiyao, and He Yiwen. Gambling equipment including a set of pai gow tiles, two dice, 50 yuan in silver dollars, and small silver and copper coins were seized. The ringleader Yin Bota and the hotel manager Dong Yaoting were arrested and taken to the police station. Yesterday, they were escorted to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. Police lawyer Yuan Jiabin stated the case, prosecuting for gambling offenses, and stating that hotel manager Dong Yaoting violated Article 6 of the Shanghai Municipal Council's Hotel Regulations, requesting legal proceedings. Evidence was presented to the court. Detective Mai Songyi reported the circumstances of the arrest. Yin Bota confessed that because of the New Year, he invited friends to open a room to have some fun, but denied gambling or taking a cut. Yin Boqing and others confessed to gambling. Dong Yaoting stated that he did not know they were gambling pai gow in the room. Judge Wu Fanglian verified the confessions and ruled that Dong Yaoting had violated the regulations and was fined 50 yuan. Yin Bota was fined 30 yuan for gambling. Each gambler was fined 10 yuan. The seized gambling equipment and funds were confiscated according to regulations.

Yi Fangshuo's Appeal to be Heard Today 190

Yi Fangshuo, a famous comedian and leader of the Jingshen Troupe from Hangzhou, residing at No. 147, Baxianfang Entrance, Huagniao Road, French Concession, and performing at the New World Company's rooftop garden, was accused of raping his cousin Yi Baozhu and arrested by the French police. Suicide Due to Economic Pressure 191

Shen Songquan, a 21-year-old silk merchant from Nanxun, committed suicide by taking poison in a room at a certain hotel at the intersection of New Bridge Street, Route Edouard VII, French Concession, due to economic pressure at 2:00 AM on New Year's Day. At 2:00 PM, the waiter urged him to get up, but there was no response. The door was opened and it was discovered that Shen had died in bed. The police were immediately notified and dispatched detectives to investigate. A wallet was found in his pocket, containing a small suicide note written in pencil, several small photos of himself, and thirty cents. Nothing else was found. The body was sent to the mortuary for examination. The next day, the Second Special Court was requested to send a prosecutor to the mortuary to verify that the deceased had died by taking poison. Since there were no family members, the body was ordered to be handed over to the Tongren Fuyuan Hall for burial. The belongings were stored in the warehouse awaiting family identification.

The East China Sea and the Taiwan Strait are overcast, with rain and strong northeasterly seasonal winds. Furthermore, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in Shanghai was 43.0 degrees at its highest and 32.9 degrees at its lowest. On the same day last year, the temperature was 54.3 degrees at its highest and 38.3 degrees at its lowest.

To the Editor: In today's (7th) local news column of your newspaper, in the news item "(The Course of the Gang's Extortion Case)," there is a statement saying "(Sheng Bingru, a native of Jingjiang, is about 40 years old and currently works as a shipbuilding technician at the Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications)." However, there was a Mr. Sheng Pinru, who was a shipbuilding engineer registered with this bureau and once worked for this bureau, but he has long since left his post and is not currently holding any position in this bureau. Please publish this letter to make a correction. Sincerely, Shanghai Navigation Administration Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, February 7.

Tense Situation 207

The jump ball in the center circle, the fierce battle began, shuttling back and forth, Yu Genxiang shot diagonally from the west corner, taking the first point for Fudan. Chen Zongqi, a Jiangwan athlete, made a comparable shot, and Zhang Wen succeeded without falling behind, taking the lead with 4-2. Main Player Fouled Out 209

Fierce Chase Ineffective 210

Southeast Women's Physical Education Teachers' School Builds a Swimming Pool 216

The Southeast Women's Physical Education Teachers' School in Jiangwan is a well-equipped physical education school in Shanghai. The facilities, sports equipment, etc., are all complete. In recent years, swimming has become increasingly popular, but there are not many public or private sports organizations in Shanghai that have swimming pools. In view of this, the school specifically purchased more than ten acres of land behind the school in Jiangwan last year. In addition to dedicating part of it to sports fields, the rest will be used as a base for building a swimming pool. After several preparations, the drawings have now been completed and bidding for construction has begun. The pool is designed to be extremely perfect, with a magnificent appearance and exquisite interior. Once completed, it will be the only complete swimming pool in Shanghai. According to the school authorities, construction of the pool will begin soon, and it is expected to be completed around mid-May, just when the weather is getting warmer and swimming is popular. The school's students are even more eager to succeed as soon as possible to show off their skills.

800,000 Yuan Allocated for Compulsory Education in the 24th Year 218

庚 款 Allocated

Ministry of Education Proposes Plan

(Nanjing, 7th dispatch) The Geng Kuan Joint Committee held its second meeting at the Executive Yuan, resolving to subsidize cultural and educational funds. Zhejiang Education Department Orders Promulgation of Measures for Waiving Entrance Exams for Outstanding Elementary School Students Attached to Provincial Schools 220

In order to encourage outstanding students in elementary schools attached to provincial secondary schools, the Zhejiang Education Department specially formulated Provisional Measures for Waiving Entrance Exams for Outstanding Graduates of Elementary Schools Attached to Zhejiang Provincial Secondary Schools and ordered them to be promulgated to all provincial junior secondary schools and schools of equivalent level to junior high schools when recruiting first-year students, following the procedures. The standards for waiving entrance exams are: 1) Academic Performance: In the graduation exam, all subjects except skill subjects must be above 70 points, and other subjects must be above 80 points. In the previous three semesters, each semester must also be above 75 points, and they must have continuously studied for four semesters in the fifth and sixth grades of an attached elementary school. 2) Conduct Performance: The conduct grade in the graduating semester must be above 80 points, and the previous three semesters must also be above 75 points. 3) Physical Education Performance: All four semesters must be above 70 points. If each school's calculation of grades does not use the percentage method, it should also be converted to a percentage grade.

The General Assembly of the National Central University Alumni Association is Postponed 221

Reported Branches Do Not Meet the Legal Number of Units

The Meeting Resolved to Postpone it to the Spring Break

The National Nanga, Dongda, and Central University Alumni Association, following the recommendations of 315 members including the Shanghai, Zhenjiang, Suzhou, Wuhan, Jinan, Kunshan, Jinhua, and Hangzhou branches, as well as members Zhou Bangdao, Chen Shizhen, Zhang Tingxiu, Zhang Su, Zhang Zhongfan, Ou Jifu, Xie Linshu, Fu Guanglin, Sun Guangyu, and Liu Zonglie, changed the system from a general membership meeting to a system of representatives from local branches. After deliberation by the Executive Committee of the association, a communication method was used to generally solicit the opinions of most local members, who expressed their support. It was decided to hold a temporary representative meeting of local branches on February 9th and 10th to discuss everything. All branches were also notified that they should elect representatives to attend the meeting in accordance with the established procedures before February 31st and report to the meeting. Since the meeting date was approaching very closely, only seven branches had reported. There are 37 branches that have been formally established, and 15 more are in the process of preparation and reorganization. In terms of formal branches, the number of attending units will be less than one-fifth. In terms of the total of 52 branches mentioned above, it is less than one-seventh. In this situation, in order to take into account the rights and interests of all members and the overall development of association affairs, the association held an emergency meeting of the Executive Committee Standing Committee at 7:30 PM yesterday (5th), resolving to postpone the temporary representative meeting to the spring break period, April 4th and 5th, to be held in Nanjing. All branch representatives who have been elected are still valid, and those who have not been elected must still follow the previously established local branch procedures for selecting representatives and matters requiring attention ten days before the conference. It is heard that a quick letter has been sent to each branch and a public notice has been published in the newspaper. The association's meeting is postponed to April 4th and 5th, which coincides with the spring break period.

Liu Tingfang Raises Three Questions About the Ten Professors' Manifesto 223

Simultaneously Expresses His Own Opinions

Advocates the Sinicization of Imported Education

｜Ten Professors Respond: No Background, Aiming to Revitalize the Nation｜Recently, Dr. Liu Tingfang, Vice President of Yenching University in Beiping and Editor of the Education Column of the Tianjin Dagongbao, visited Shanghai and visited the people who signed the "Ten Professors' Manifesto" to discuss the manifesto. The record of their conversation is as follows:

When the professors saw Mr. Liu visiting, they immediately asked him to express his opinions on the Ten Professors' Manifesto. Mr. Liu said that we have been old friends for many years, and now I will impolitely raise three questions first, requesting answers: 1) Does this Chinese-based cultural construction movement have a political background? 2) What attitude do you take towards the issue of cultural control? 3) What is the ultimate goal of this movement? I hope you can explain it simply so that I can answer inquiries from friends after returning north.

The professors replied: 1) Our Ten Professors' Manifesto is purely based on personal relationships. From an academic standpoint, we have expressed some common opinions of the ten of us. Not only does our action have no background, but it also does not represent the institutions served by the ten of us. However, since the manifesto was published, not only have leaders from all walks of life across the country expressed considerable sympathy and given us a lot of guidance, but the authorities have also given us an opportunity to develop freely because our movement is purely academic.

2) The Ten Professors' Manifesto is nothing more than expressing a foolish opinion based on the idea that everyone is responsible for the rise and fall of the country, asking the people of the country for guidance. This has absolutely nothing to do with the issue of cultural control. We believe that if we can gather experts from all over the country to discuss opinions on building a Chinese-based culture, come up with a result, and seek a way to revitalize the nation for everyone to refer to, it seems like a worthwhile thing to do. 3) Our ultimate goal is, of course, to revitalize the nation, that is, how to build a Chinese-based culture in order to achieve the revival of the Chinese nation. The Japanese often say that modern international warfare is a competition of national intelligence. We believe that not only is warfare like this, but the modern struggle for national survival is also the same. Therefore, our foolish opinion is that the construction of a Chinese-based culture is a work that cannot be delayed.

Mr. Liu continued that he has been engaged in education for many years and is also a member of the Tomorrow Education Society. That education society advocates: 1) The original Chinese education should be further advanced to make it scientific and productive. 2) All foreign education should be Sinicized. The so-called Sinicization is to adapt to current needs and be constantly updated, not to go back to the old paper piles to make a living. 3) The education cause should gather ideas and benefit widely, and should not be monopolized by one faction. Because he has this view, he can generally agree with the Ten Professors' Manifesto. However, he said that since he believes in Christianity, he recognizes religion as part of culture and cannot exclude it. Moreover, there is a considerable need in the work of revitalizing the nation, but it should also be Sinicized. Finally, Mr. Liu also promised that after returning north, he would convey the meaning of the ten people to his friends in the north. It is heard that Mr. Liu has already returned to Beiping by taking the Pinghu through train that afternoon.
