Shen Bao Local Supplement Film Special Issue

The Past and Future of the Outdated Hollywood Queen, Pola Negri, Returns to Hollywood 270

— Yi Min

I'm afraid no one can remember this outdated Hollywood queen, Pola Negri. She has been retired for almost two years since she starred in "A Woman Commands." Most people assume that she will live a leisurely life in the forest from now on and will no longer enter the film industry.

However, her long history in Hollywood makes her unwilling to abandon it for a long time. People familiar with the anecdotes of the film industry know that she was the pioneer of the Hollywood glamorous style. Greta Garbo is just a latecomer, so Hollywood people who admire her are very sorry for her departure and believe that she will not go and never return.

She was also one of those who could not make sound films because she had not learned English. She is Polish. When she was selected as the queen in Hollywood, many people went to congratulate her, but she could only extend the back of her hand for people to shake. After she acted A Woman Commands, she went to Europe. In these two years, she learned fluent English and returned to Hollywood. The news of her revitalization spread out and alarmed many people in the film industry.

Pola Negri is now not young. In the past, she was the woman in the film industry who was most deeply in love, and she had fallen into the web of love many times. Charlie Chaplin was also one of the people she was madly in love with. Many people said that Chaplin and her were married, but this rumor has not been clearly confirmed. At that time, she frankly announced that it was because of Chaplin that she stayed in Hollywood for a long time.

The most unforgettable thing for most people is the story between her and Valentino. At that time, people talked a lot, saying that Pola's heart only contained one Valentino, but unfortunately, Valentino died young. The person who cried most sadly in front of his spirit and fainted was Pola Negri. It can be seen that Pola did have a considerable relationship with Valentino.

However, Pola has been married several times. Prince Mivarana is also one of her divorced husbands. In addition, William Hayes, Roth Laroque, etc. were once her lovers. Her life is like a drama. Looking back on the paintings, she once resolved to compile her experiences into a movie script in the era of silent films, but in fact, she did not succeed.

Will Pola, who has returned to the film industry, be able to continue her past reputation? This is what Hollywood people are eager to discuss.

Many people believe that Pola is a person who bravely retreats. Five years ago, she was the first-class popular actress in the film industry. Even seniors like Garbo, Clara Bow, and Joan Crawford all willingly surrendered to her. What she felt lacking was that she could not speak English. After the sound film dominated the film industry, Hollywood made her understand her shortcomings. She could not have the slightest hesitation. Then, her return to Hollywood must have a considerable certainty, which is no need to worry about.

In the history of Hollywood, she was the one who created the glamorous style. Now the glamorous style has already undergone a sweeping movement and gradually declined. Perhaps her return to the film industry will change her previous style. It is not known.

Some people also said that Pola sighed extremely at the death of Hollywood's old queen, Mary Trancho, and often showed her intention to return to the screen. Perhaps she will want to take Mary Trancho's place and replace her.

Although Pola's future after her return is mysterious, the general public has great hope for her!

Film Review

Review of "The Red Sheep Heroic Tales" 271

— You Jing

| Carlton Theater Showing

Until now, Chinese literary and artistic writers have not yet produced a work that adequately expresses the passionate and tragic historical facts of the (Hong Yang Rebellion).

This film, "The Red Sheep Heroic Tales," like all previous poems, dramas, and essays about the (Taiping Heavenly Kingdom), does not essentially grasp the core of this great national liberation movement. It only superficially adopts some external scenes. From the perspective of (heroes creating the times), it vaguely portrays Hong Xiuquan, Yang Xiuqing, etc., as (extraordinary heroes and chivalrous figures), neglecting the masses who are the main foundation of this movement. We know that Hong Yang and others were not supermen, not figures who relied on personal power to initiate an era and open up the world, but rather figures who infused a large amount of mass will before they could exert their personal abilities. Serafimovich analyzed Guo Ruhe in (The Iron Flood) like this: (Guo Ruhe is a hero, and also not a hero, because if the masses do not regard him as their leader, if the masses do not instill ideas in him, then he is a most ordinary person. At the same time, he is also a hero, because the masses not only instill ideas in him, but also follow him and obey him as if obeying a leader).

Naturally, the film (The Red Sheep Heroic Tales) does touch upon the masses to a considerable extent, but it also abandons them. For example, when the masses were brutally exploited by officials, Hong and Feng turned their horses around to find Zhu Jiutao; they were ignored by the starving people in the famine relief ranks; Yang Xiuqing abandoned the two thousand stoneworkers and left; the masses rescued Wei Changhui from the soldiers in public outrage, but Wei said, (Thank you all, now the matter has become big, you can all disperse), etc. In several places, the author unintentionally portrays Hong Xiuquan and others as opportunistic figures.

Similarly, because they want to write about heroes by separating them from the masses, they introduce and exaggerate the heroes' surroundings with one scene after another, asking the audience to watch a series of scenes like a running account.

The stoneworkers scene is great and meaningful, if it could be organically applied throughout the film. I think if we compose a better song than Xu Zhimo's (Song of the Stoneworker) to sing, its power could be compared to the (Boatman's Song) in (Soul of the Party Member).

Perhaps to give Wang Huchen, who plays Wei Changhui, more screen time, the scene of Li Dianyuan whipping him is intensified. It's a pity that Wei is so unheroic and obediently tied up and beaten that the audience almost suspects he is a coward. This contradicts Wei's character and spoils the scene.

Finally, I must sincerely advise the author and the audience that in this time of national crisis for the Chinese nation, (The Red Sheep Heroic Tales), which reminds us of the national salvation movement, is worthy of respect.

A Scene from (Congratulations on Getting Rich) || Great Shanghai Theater Showing

Review of "Babes in Toyland" 272

— Hua Lun

Babes in Toyland

| Nanjing Theater Showing |

A comedy that mixes reality and fantasy - that is the essence of the film (Babes in Toyland). Films of this type are somewhat close to the ideals of children, and they must clearly oppose good and evil and subjectively resolve them; in other words, the ultimate opposition of good and evil is the victory of good and the defeat of evil.

What exists in the human world is often the tyranny of evildoers, and these evildoers are often impossible to eliminate. Therefore, what exists in the consciousness of ordinary people is the desire to have some kind of power to eliminate these evildoers, which constitutes their fantasy. In the world of fantasy, evildoers can certainly be eliminated.

The theme of (Babes in Toyland) is to use fantasy to solve the injustices of reality. It constructs a world of toys (Toyland), in which Mother Goose, the Three Little Pigs, the Cat Musician, Widow Peep and her daughter, the boy Tom Piper, and two toymakers live peacefully. But because of the bully Barnaby, their peace is disturbed. Barnaby uses his debt to force Peep's daughter to marry him. Peep and her daughter naturally don't want to, but they have no way to repay his debt. The two toymakers try their best but to no avail, and finally they have to agree to marry him. The two toymakers then try to disguise themselves as the bride, so they can tear up the debt agreement. But the bully tries to frame Tom Piper, saying that he killed the Little Pigs, and is sentenced to exile to (Bogeyland), and the daughter follows him. But this slanderous plot is revealed by the toymakers, and the bully escapes to (Bogeyland), and the toymakers also chase after him. Later, they escape back from Bogeyland, and the bully leads a large group of bogeymen to attack Toyland. Fortunately, the toymakers start the mechanism of the wooden soldiers, eliminating all the evil soldiers and generals, and the bully is also killed. Then, the toy world returns to peace.

Although this film still contains some confused elements, it is a very beautiful comedy, and it is bound to be welcomed by a wide audience of young people (that is, adults as well). The directors Gus Meins and Charles Rogers are also worthy of our admiration. He arranges the atmosphere of the opening fairy tale world very well. The connection of the entire film is also very appropriate, and there are no omissions in the correspondence of various events before and after, such as the toy soldiers, such as Stanner's superb skills. These are all foreshadowed very well.

In terms of acting, Laurel and Hardy are still as we expect them to be. Although they are pitiful in many places and suffer losses, they are still very enthusiastic. This spirit is fully expressed. We can discover in them human love and the passion for fighting the evil world. On the contrary, Henry Kleinbach's representation of the evil side is also appropriately expressed. His sly smile and his insidious nature make us understand him very clearly.

In short, (Babes in Toyland) can be said to be a very successful comedy film, and it is more suitable for children to appreciate.

Film Novel

The Remains of a Block of Meat (David Copperfield) ㈡ 273

— Liu Cun

When David saw the black panther, he immediately wanted to turn around and run away. He wanted to escape to Old Peggotty, Ham, and Emily, or anywhere. He wanted to leave this once harmonious, love-filled family immediately. Although he was still young, he already felt that the air in the house was completely different. His mother, who was originally gentle, happy, and very fond of him, now did not hold him in her arms, but looked shyly at Murdstone. He only heard Murdstone calling his mother's name and saying, (Clara, my love, you must remember! You must tidy yourself up. David, child, how are you?)

Once again, another stranger walked in, but the tense atmosphere in the house did not relax at all. It was a woman with a frosty face, dressed in black. Her two thick black eyebrows were connected above her nose. David's mother told him that it was Miss Murdstone, his new aunt. The new aunt then glared at David and estimated him before saying, (Generally speaking, I don't like boys. Child, how are you?) David answered briefly. His childish anger swelled in his chest. Miss Murdstone said angrily, (Such an impolite child!) She then said to his mother, (Clara, you are a beautiful and unthinking person, and you are not good at managing the family. Please give me the keys to the house.)

At this moment, David felt that he could no longer bear it. His mother, his kind and lovely mother, was with these people, like this! The air in the whole house had changed, and there was no laughter in it anymore. He soon discovered that everything, everything had changed. And he could no longer sleep in his mother's room. He spent very little time with his mother during the day. In the evening, he recited his lessons not only to her alone, but Mr. and Miss Murdstone also sat together. This made him unable to recite his lessons, because those two cold eyes stared at him, causing his memory to disappear. So, every time the result was that he had to cry bitterly. His mother also cried for him, begging Mr. Murdstone to forgive his youth and ignorance.

But Murdstone simply would not forgive him. He dragged David into his own room and beat him with a stick as if he were a dog who disobeyed his master's orders. David cried and pleaded, (Mr. Murdstone, sir, no! Please don't hit me! Sir, I will remember. If I am with my mother, I will definitely remember, but when you and Miss Murdstone are watching me, I can't recite it. I really can't recite it.)

Mr. Murdstone waved the stick in his face and said, (Really, David? Let's try it.) As he said, he hit him hard. David could not bear the pain in his body and the shame he felt in his heart for a moment. The anger in his little mind suddenly erupted. He slammed his head straight into Mr. Murdstone and bit his hand hard with his teeth. At this time, the door was locked, and his mother could not get in. She cried and begged outside the door.

David was locked in the room, and no one was allowed to see him. He always heard strange, low voices speaking outside the room. Finally, Peggotty secretly walked to his door and told him in a low voice that he would soon have a little brother or sister. He pounded on the door, begging them to let him out. But now no one paid attention to him anymore. Later, the door suddenly opened. Like a poor little dog, he crawled downstairs and walked into that silent and gloomy room. He finally found Peggotty, who told him, (Your mother, that lovely baby···he is···) David said quietly, (She is dead.) Peggotty said, (Your little brother, poor little thing, he is also dead···) (To be continued)
